## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    subgraph Deployment
        subgraph Pod
            subgraph Container[Controller Container]
                Env[Environment Variables]
                Ports[Exposed Ports]
                Probes[Health Checks]
            end
            Volumes[Mounted Volumes]
        end
    end
    Env --> CLUSTER[Cluster Config]
    Env --> WEBHOOK[Webhook Config]
    Env --> METRICS[Metrics Config]
    Env --> FEATURES[Feature Gates]
    Ports --> MetricsPort[8080: Metrics]
    Ports --> WebhookPort[Webhook Port]
    Ports --> HealthPort[Health Probe]
    Probes --> Liveness[/healthz]
    Probes --> Readiness[/readyz]
    Volumes --> ConfigLog[config-logging]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> DeploymentCreated
    DeploymentCreated --> PodScheduling
    PodScheduling --> ContainerStarting
    ContainerStarting --> SecurityContextApplied
    SecurityContextApplied --> EnvironmentLoaded
    EnvironmentLoaded --> PortsExposed
    PortsExposed --> LivenessCheck
    LivenessCheck --> ReadinessCheck
    ReadinessCheck --> Running
    Running --> HealthMonitoring
    HealthMonitoring --> Running
    Running --> [*]
```
